=== Iteration 1 - [2026-05-01 18:52:46] ===
PLAN:
  === ADJUSTED ENVIRONMENT SETUP PLAN (CPU-ONLY, x86_64, No GPU) ===
  1. DOWNLOADS NEEDED:
     - Docker (version 28.1.1 already available, meets requirements; minimum as per [Docker docs](https://docs.docker.com/get-docker/))
     - Curl (latest stable, or system package manager version)
     - Gum (latest release, [gum repo](https://github.com/charmbracelet/gum))
     - jq (latest stable, or system package manager version)
     - Python 3 (minimum 3.7) and pip3 (for Python libraries)
     - **(REMOVED)** Nvidia drivers & CUDA toolkit (not required; no NVIDIA GPU)
     - **(REMOVED)** Nvidia Container Toolkit (not required; no NVIDIA GPU)
     - WSL2 (for Windows, if not on native Linux/macOS)
     - **(REMOVED)** Rosetta 2 (not required; x86_64 architecture)
     - Nesa bootstrap script: https://raw.githubusercontent.com/nesaorg/bootstrap/master/bootstrap.sh
     - (Optional) Hugging Face API key (user to obtain from https://huggingface.co/settings/tokens)
     - (Optional) NES testnet tokens (user to obtain from https://beta.nesa.ai/faucet)
  2. FILES TO CREATE:
     - `~/.nesa/env/base.env`
       - Content: Node moniker, referral code, public IP, other node identity info.
     - `~/.nesa/env/orchestrator.env`
       - Content: secp256k1 private key (imported or generated), node ID, Hugging Face API key.
     - `~/.nesa/logs/bootstrap.log`
       - Content: All bootstrap script activity, session logs.
     - (On first run, these files are auto-generated/updated by the bootstrap script. User can edit if needed for "advanced setup.")
  3. NECESSARY TEST CASES IN THE CODEBASE:
     - System Prerequisite Checks:
       - Test for Docker, curl, gum, jq, Python3, and OS compatibility.
       - **(REMOVED)** NVIDIA checks (no GPU; fallback to CPU-only mode always)
     - Wallet Management:
       - Generate new secp256k1 wallet and verify keypair format.
       - Import existing private key and validate correctness.
       - Store private key securely and verify file permissions.
     - NES Balance & Deposit:
       - Query NES wallet balance (offline and online/testnet scenarios).
       - Validate deposit transaction and minimum requirement enforcement.
       - Handle faucet requests (testnet).
     - On-Chain Registration:
       - Register node/miner and verify automatic retry logic.
       - Check node registration status.
     - Node Lifecycle Management:
       - Start, stop, pause, resume node containers.
       - Node deletion cleans up all containers, configs, and data.
     - GPU/CPU Detection:
       - **(MODIFIED)** Always fallback to CPU-only mode; skip GPU/NVIDIA setup.
       - Validate node runs on CPU; ensure Docker images do not include CUDA/nvidia dependencies.
     - Logging & Dashboard:
       - Log all activities to ~/.nesa/logs/bootstrap.log.
       - Live log streaming and status dashboard access.
     - Auto-Update Mechanism:
       - Test automatic update pull and container restart.
     - Configuration Edge Cases:
       - Re-running bootstrap script with existing configuration.
       - Editing config files directly and auto-detection by script.
  4. COMPLETE TODO LIST:
     1. Update the OS and install all necessary package managers (apt, yum, brew, choco as appropriate).
        - Verify: Run `lsb_release -a` or `uname -a` to confirm OS.
        - **(RECOMMENDED)** Ensure OS is compatible with x86_64 Docker images (e.g., Ubuntu 20.04, Debian Bullseye).
     2. Docker install step: **Skip if Docker 28.1.1 is already present and functional.**
        - Verify: `docker --version` is 28.1.1, `docker info` shows BuildKit and compose support.
     3. Install curl, gum, jq, and Python3/pip3.
        - Verify: `curl --version`, `gum --version`, `jq --version`, `python3 --version`
     4. **(REMOVED)** NVIDIA GPU steps:
        - Skip installation of NVIDIA drivers, CUDA toolkit, and Nvidia Container Toolkit.
        - **(MODIFIED VERIFY)** Confirm `nvidia-smi` is NOT required, and no Docker images use `--gpus` flag.
     5. **(REMOVED)** Apple Silicon (ARM64) steps:
        - Skip Rosetta 2 installation and ARM64-specific instructions.
     6. For Windows:
        - Install WSL2 and a compatible Linux distribution.
        - Verify: `wsl --list --online` and `wsl uname -a`
     7. Download the Nesa bootstrap script:
        - `curl -O https://raw.githubusercontent.com/nesaorg/bootstrap/master/bootstrap.sh`
        - Make executable: `chmod +x bootstrap.sh`
        - Verify: Script present and executable.
     8. Run the bootstrap script:
        - `bash bootstrap.sh` or `bash <(curl -s https://raw.githubusercontent.com/nesaorg/bootstrap/master/bootstrap.sh)`
        - Follow prompts for node name, referral code, Hugging Face API key, wallet setup.
        - Verify: No errors in script output.
     9. Generate or import a secp256k1 wallet/private key as prompted.
        - Save private key securely.
        - Verify: `~/.nesa/env/orchestrator.env` contains the correct key.
     10. Obtain NES tokens (from faucet for testnet).
         - Verify: Script can query and display NES balance.
     11. Complete on-chain registration and deposit step.
         - Verify: Registration confirmed and deposit status OK.
     12. Start the Nesa node (containers start automatically if previous steps succeeded).
         - Verify: `docker ps` shows containers running.
         - **(MODIFIED)** Ensure containers are running CPU-compatible images only (e.g., ubuntu:20.04, python:3.10-slim).
         - **(RECOMMENDED)** Use `--platform=linux/amd64` if building/pulling images explicitly.
     13. Access node status dashboard and live logs via script menu.
         - Verify: No errors, accurate status, and logs appear.
     14. Test node lifecycle (start, stop, pause, resume) and deletion.
         - Verify: Containers respond accordingly; deletion removes all config/data.
     15. (Optional) Edit config files in `~/.nesa/env/` and re-run script to confirm detection of changes.
         - Verify: Script skips wizard and loads existing configuration.
     16. Add user to Docker group (if permission errors occur):
         - `sudo usermod -aG docker $USER && newgrp docker`
         - Verify: Able to run `docker` commands without sudo.
     17. (If errors): Consult logs in `~/.nesa/logs/bootstrap.log` and follow troubleshooting steps.
         - Verify: Errors documented, able to resolve with guide.
     18. (Optional) Join Discord and explore GitBook documentation for further support.
         - Verify: Able to access resources and ask community questions.
  5. ADDITIONAL COMPATIBILITY NOTES:
     - All Docker images and containers must specify or default to `--platform=linux/amd64` to ensure x86_64 compatibility.
     - Do not use any CUDA, nvidia/cuda, or GPU-specific base images or instructions.
     - Ensure memory and storage requirements are met (large RAM available—no explicit limits needed).
     - Working directory is `/home/cc/EnvGym/data/20260501_153628_tensorblock_gpt-4.1/nesa_bootstrap`; confirm script and containers use correct paths and do not assume root or home directory only.
     - extfs/overlay2 storage driver is supported and compatible; confirm Docker uses overlay2 if possible.
     - All instructions and scripts should be compatible with Linux (Ubuntu/Debian recommended), macOS (Intel), and Windows with WSL2.
     - Validate base images used in Dockerfiles: ubuntu:20.04, python:3.10-slim, debian:bullseye (amd64 variants only).
  6. SUMMARY OF CHANGES:
     - All GPU/NVIDIA/CUDA-related steps, checks, and downloads have been removed.
     - Rosetta/ARM-specific steps removed (system is x86_64).
     - All Docker images and instructions are confirmed as compatible with x86_64.
     - Ensure fallback and detection logic always defaults to CPU-only mode.
     - Storage and memory notes confirm no special limits or requirements.
     - Path and directory notes added for deep working directory compatibility.
     - Docker version and features are confirmed as fully supported.

NEXT:
  current progress
  - The adjusted environment setup plan has been fully defined for CPU-only, x86_64, and no-GPU systems.
  - Docker version 28.1.1 is confirmed as available and compatible.
  - The Dockerfile attempts to use ubuntu:20.04 with a specific sha256 digest as the base image.
  - The Docker build failed because the specified sha256 digest for ubuntu:20.04 could not be resolved (image not found on Docker Hub).
  - All subsequent Dockerfile steps were not executed due to the build failure.
  next step
  - Modify the Dockerfile to use the standard ubuntu:20.04 image (remove the @sha256:... digest) as the base image:
    ```dockerfile
    FROM ubuntu:20.04
    ```
  - Re-run the Docker build to verify successful image pull and execution of subsequent build steps.
  - If image integrity verification is required, use a valid and existing sha256 digest from Docker Hub for ubuntu:20.04.

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04@sha256:7e4e1b4d7ce7ef3c5da2b1c2e7f3f1b8e4a1e3a5cf0a9f6f8d9a4f2e2a2a3c4b
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONIOENCODING=utf-8
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get upgrade -y && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
        curl \
        jq \
        python3 \
        python3-pip \
        ca-certificates \
        git \
        lsb-release \
        sudo \
        bash \
        build-essential \
        wget && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install gum (latest release)
  RUN GUM_VERSION=$(curl -s https://api.github.com/repos/charmbracelet/gum/releases/latest | jq -r '.tag_name') && \
      ARCH=amd64 && \
      wget -q https://github.com/charmbracelet/gum/releases/download/${GUM_VERSION}/gum_${GUM_VERSION}_linux_${ARCH}.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf gum_${GUM_VERSION}_linux_${ARCH}.tar.gz && \
      mv gum /usr/local/bin/gum && \
      rm gum_${GUM_VERSION}_linux_${ARCH}.tar.gz
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set working directory to repository root
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/20260501_153628_tensorblock_gpt-4.1/nesa_bootstrap
  # Copy repository contents (assumes Docker build context is repository root)
  COPY . .
  # Download Nesa bootstrap script and make it executable
  RUN curl -O https://raw.githubusercontent.com/nesaorg/bootstrap/master/bootstrap.sh && \
      chmod +x bootstrap.sh
  # Create necessary directories for Nesa environment and logs
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.nesa/env /root/.nesa/logs
  # Ensure overlay2 storage driver is used if available (for tests, not enforced)
  RUN if docker info | grep -q 'overlay2'; then echo "overlay2 storage driver supported"; else echo "overlay2 storage driver not detected"; fi || true
  # Set default shell to bash and launch interactive CLI at container start
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONIOENCODING=utf-8

  # Copy repository contents (assumes Docker build context is repository root)
  COPY . .
  # Download Nesa bootstrap script and make it executable
  RUN curl -O https://raw.githubusercontent.com/nesaorg/bootstrap/master/bootstrap.sh && \
      chmod +x bootstrap.sh
  # Create necessary directories for Nesa environment and logs
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.nesa/env /root/.nesa/logs
  # Ensure overlay2 storage driver is used if available (for tests, not enforced)
  RUN if docker info | grep -q 'overlay2'; then echo "overlay2 storage driver supported"; else echo "overlay2 storage driver not detected"; fi || true
  # Set default shell to bash and launch interactive CLI at container start
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONIOENCODING=utf-8
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get upgrade -y && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
        curl \
        jq \
        python3 \
        python3-pip \
        ca-certificates \
        git \
        lsb-release \
        sudo \
        bash \
        build-essential \
        wget \
        tar && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install gum (latest release) with debug info and correct binary extraction
  RUN set -ex && \
      GUM_VERSION=$(curl -s https://api.github.com/repos/charmbracelet/gum/releases/latest | jq -r '.tag_name') && \
      ARCH=amd64 && \
      wget -O gum.tar.gz https://github.com/charmbracelet/gum/releases/download/${GUM_VERSION}/gum_${GUM_VERSION}_linux_${ARCH}.tar.gz && \
      mkdir -p /tmp/gum && \
      tar -xzf gum.tar.gz -C /tmp/gum && \
      mv /tmp/gum/gum /usr/local/bin/gum && \
      rm -rf gum.tar.gz /tmp/gum
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set working directory to repository root
  WORKDIR /nesa_bootstrap
  # Copy repository contents (assumes Docker build context is repository root)
  COPY . .
  # Download Nesa bootstrap script and make it executable
  RUN curl -O https://raw.githubusercontent.com/nesaorg/bootstrap/master/bootstrap.sh && \
      chmod +x bootstrap.sh
  # Create necessary directories for Nesa environment and logs
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.nesa/env /root/.nesa/logs
  # Ensure overlay2 storage driver is used if available (for tests, not enforced)
  RUN if docker info | grep -q 'overlay2'; then echo "overlay2 storage driver supported"; else echo "overlay2 storage driver not detected"; fi || true
  # Set default shell to bash and launch interactive CLI at container start
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONIOENCODING=utf-8
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get upgrade -y && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
        curl \
        jq \
        python3 \
        python3-pip \
        ca-certificates \
        git \
        lsb-release \
        sudo \
        bash \
        build-essential \
        wget \
        tar && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install gum (fixed version, with debug info, and robust URL handling)
  RUN set -ex && \
      GUM_VERSION="v0.13.0" && \
      ARCH=amd64 && \
      GUM_FILENAME="gum_${GUM_VERSION#v}_linux_${ARCH}.tar.gz" && \
      GUM_URL="https://github.com/charmbracelet/gum/releases/download/${GUM_VERSION}/${GUM_FILENAME}" && \
      echo "Using gum version: $GUM_VERSION" && \
      echo "Download URL: $GUM_URL" && \
      wget -O gum.tar.gz "$GUM_URL" && \
      mkdir -p /tmp/gum && \
      tar -xzf gum.tar.gz -C /tmp/gum && \
      mv /tmp/gum/gum /usr/local/bin/gum && \
      rm -rf gum.tar.gz /tmp/gum
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set working directory to repository root
  WORKDIR /nesa_bootstrap
  # Copy repository contents (assumes Docker build context is repository root)
  COPY . .
  # Download Nesa bootstrap script and make it executable
  RUN curl -O https://raw.githubusercontent.com/nesaorg/bootstrap/master/bootstrap.sh && \
      chmod +x bootstrap.sh
  # Create necessary directories for Nesa environment and logs
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.nesa/env /root/.nesa/logs
  # Ensure overlay2 storage driver is used if available (for tests, not enforced)
  RUN if docker info | grep -q 'overlay2'; then echo "overlay2 storage driver supported"; else echo "overlay2 storage driver not detected"; fi || true
  # Set default shell to bash and launch interactive CLI at container start
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONIOENCODING=utf-8
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get upgrade -y && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
        curl \
        jq \
        python3 \
        python3-pip \
        ca-certificates \
        git \
        lsb-release \
        sudo \
        bash \
        build-essential \
        wget \
        tar && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install gum (fixed version, with debug info, and robust URL handling)
  RUN set -ex && \
      GUM_VERSION="v0.13.0" && \
      ARCH=amd64 && \
      GUM_FILENAME="gum_${GUM_VERSION#v}_linux_${ARCH}.tar.gz" && \
      GUM_URL="https://github.com/charmbracelet/gum/releases/download/${GUM_VERSION}/${GUM_FILENAME}" && \
      echo "Using gum version: $GUM_VERSION" && \
      echo "Download URL: $GUM_URL" && \
      wget -O gum.tar.gz "$GUM_URL" && \
      mkdir -p /tmp/gum && \
      tar -xzf gum.tar.gz -C /tmp/gum && \
      ls -al /tmp/gum && \
      if [ ! -f /tmp/gum/gum ]; then echo "gum binary not found in tarball extraction"; exit 1; fi && \
      mv /tmp/gum/gum /usr/local/bin/gum && \
      chmod +x /usr/local/bin/gum && \
      /usr/local/bin/gum --version && \
      rm -rf gum.tar.gz /tmp/gum
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set working directory to repository root
  WORKDIR /nesa_bootstrap
  # Copy repository contents (assumes Docker build context is repository root)
  COPY . .
  # Download Nesa bootstrap script and make it executable
  RUN curl -O https://raw.githubusercontent.com/nesaorg/bootstrap/master/bootstrap.sh && \
      chmod +x bootstrap.sh
  # Create necessary directories for Nesa environment and logs
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.nesa/env /root/.nesa/logs
  # Ensure overlay2 storage driver is used if available (for tests, not enforced)
  RUN if command -v docker >/dev/null 2>&1; then \
        if docker info | grep -q 'overlay2'; then echo "overlay2 storage driver supported"; else echo "overlay2 storage driver not detected"; fi; \
      else \
        echo "docker command not found, skipping overlay2 check"; \
      fi || true
  # Set default shell to bash and launch interactive CLI at container start
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONIOENCODING=utf-8
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get upgrade -y && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
        curl \
        jq \
        python3 \
        python3-pip \
        ca-certificates \
        git \
        lsb-release \
        sudo \
        bash \
        build-essential \
        wget \
        tar && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install gum (fixed version, with debug info, and robust URL handling)
  RUN set -ex && \
      GUM_VERSION="v0.13.0" && \
      ARCH=amd64 && \
      GUM_FILENAME="gum_${GUM_VERSION#v}_linux_${ARCH}.tar.gz" && \
      GUM_URL="https://github.com/charmbracelet/gum/releases/download/${GUM_VERSION}/${GUM_FILENAME}" && \
      echo "Using gum version: $GUM_VERSION" && \
      echo "Download URL: $GUM_URL" && \
      wget -O gum.tar.gz "$GUM_URL" && \
      mkdir -p /tmp/gum && \
      tar -xzf gum.tar.gz -C /tmp/gum && \
      ls -alR /tmp/gum && \
      GUM_BIN_PATH=$(find /tmp/gum -type f -name gum | head -n 1) && \
      if [ -z "$GUM_BIN_PATH" ]; then echo "gum binary not found in tarball extraction"; exit 1; fi && \
      mv "$GUM_BIN_PATH" /usr/local/bin/gum && \
      chmod +x /usr/local/bin/gum && \
      /usr/local/bin/gum --version && \
      rm -rf gum.tar.gz /tmp/gum
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set working directory to repository root
  WORKDIR /nesa_bootstrap
  # Copy repository contents (assumes Docker build context is repository root)
  COPY . .
  # Download Nesa bootstrap script and make it executable
  RUN curl -O https://raw.githubusercontent.com/nesaorg/bootstrap/master/bootstrap.sh && \
      chmod +x bootstrap.sh
  # Create necessary directories for Nesa environment and logs
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.nesa/env /root/.nesa/logs
  # Ensure overlay2 storage driver is used if available (for tests, not enforced)
  RUN if command -v docker >/dev/null 2>&1; then \
        if docker info | grep -q 'overlay2'; then echo "overlay2 storage driver supported"; else echo "overlay2 storage driver not detected"; fi; \
      else \
        echo "docker command not found, skipping overlay2 check"; \
      fi || true
  # Set default shell to bash and launch interactive CLI at container start
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

    - Replace the `tar -xzf gum.tar.gz && mv gum /usr/local/bin/gum` line with the following two lines to reliably move the binary regardless of extraction structure:
      ```
      tar -xzf gum.tar.gz
      find . -type f -name gum -exec mv {} /usr/local/bin/gum \;
      ```
    - Then proceed with `chmod +x /usr/local/bin/gum` as before.

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONIOENCODING=utf-8
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get upgrade -y && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
        curl \
        jq \
        python3 \
        python3-pip \
        ca-certificates \
        git \
        lsb-release \
        sudo \
        bash \
        build-essential \
        wget \
        tar && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install gum (fixed version, correctly handle tarball structure)
  RUN set -ex && \
      GUM_VERSION="v0.13.0" && \
      ARCH=amd64 && \
      GUM_FILENAME="gum_${GUM_VERSION#v}_linux_${ARCH}.tar.gz" && \
      GUM_URL="https://github.com/charmbracelet/gum/releases/download/${GUM_VERSION}/${GUM_FILENAME}" && \
      wget -O gum.tar.gz "$GUM_URL" && \
      tar -xzf gum.tar.gz && \
      mv gum /usr/local/bin/gum && \
      chmod +x /usr/local/bin/gum && \
      /usr/local/bin/gum --version && \
      rm -rf gum.tar.gz
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set working directory to repository root
  WORKDIR /nesa_bootstrap
  # Copy repository contents (assumes Docker build context is repository root)
  COPY . .
  # Download Nesa bootstrap script and make it executable
  RUN curl -O https://raw.githubusercontent.com/nesaorg/bootstrap/master/bootstrap.sh && \
      chmod +x bootstrap.sh
  # Create necessary directories for Nesa environment and logs
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.nesa/env /root/.nesa/logs
  # Ensure overlay2 storage driver is used if available (for tests, not enforced)
  RUN if command -v docker >/dev/null 2>&1; then \
        if docker info | grep -q 'overlay2'; then echo "overlay2 storage driver supported"; else echo "overlay2 storage driver not detected"; fi; \
      else \
        echo "docker command not found, skipping overlay2 check"; \
      fi || true
  # Set default shell to bash and launch interactive CLI at container start
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONIOENCODING=utf-8
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get upgrade -y && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
        curl \
        jq \
        python3 \
        python3-pip \
        ca-certificates \
        git \
        lsb-release \
        sudo \
        bash \
        build-essential \
        wget \
        tar && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install gum (fixed version, correctly handle tarball structure)
  RUN set -ex && \
      GUM_VERSION="v0.13.0" && \
      ARCH=amd64 && \
      GUM_FILENAME="gum_${GUM_VERSION#v}_linux_${ARCH}.tar.gz" && \
      GUM_URL="https://github.com/charmbracelet/gum/releases/download/${GUM_VERSION}/${GUM_FILENAME}" && \
      wget -O gum.tar.gz "$GUM_URL" && \
      tar -xzf gum.tar.gz && \
      find . -type f -name gum -exec mv {} /usr/local/bin/gum \; && \
      chmod +x /usr/local/bin/gum && \
      /usr/local/bin/gum --version && \
      rm -rf gum.tar.gz
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set working directory to repository root
  WORKDIR /nesa_bootstrap
  # Copy repository contents (assumes Docker build context is repository root)
  COPY . .
  # Download Nesa bootstrap script and make it executable
  RUN curl -O https://raw.githubusercontent.com/nesaorg/bootstrap/master/bootstrap.sh && \
      chmod +x bootstrap.sh
  # Create necessary directories for Nesa environment and logs
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.nesa/env /root/.nesa/logs
  # Ensure overlay2 storage driver is used if available (for tests, not enforced)
  RUN if command -v docker >/dev/null 2>&1; then \
        if docker info | grep -q 'overlay2'; then echo "overlay2 storage driver supported"; else echo "overlay2 storage driver not detected"; fi; \
      else \
        echo "docker command not found, skipping overlay2 check"; \
      fi || true
  # Set default shell to bash and launch interactive CLI at container start
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

      GUM_FILENAME="gum_${GUM_VERSION#v}_linux_${ARCH}.tar.gz" && \
      GUM_URL="https://github.com/charmbracelet/gum/releases/download/${GUM_VERSION}/${GUM_FILENAME}" && \
      wget -O gum.tar.gz "$GUM_URL" && \
      tar -xzf gum.tar.gz && \
      mv gum_*_linux_amd64/gum /usr/local/bin/gum && \
      chmod +x /usr/local/bin/gum && \
      /usr/local/bin/gum --version && \
      rm -rf gum.tar.gz gum_*_linux_amd64
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set working directory to repository root
  WORKDIR /nesa_bootstrap
  # Copy repository contents (assumes Docker build context is repository root)
  COPY . .
  # Download Nesa bootstrap script and make it executable
  RUN curl -O https://raw.githubusercontent.com/nesaorg/bootstrap/master/bootstrap.sh && \
      chmod +x bootstrap.sh
  # Create necessary directories for Nesa environment and logs
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.nesa/env /root/.nesa/logs
  # Ensure overlay2 storage driver is used if available (for tests, not enforced)
  RUN if command -v docker >/dev/null 2>&1; then \
        if docker info | grep -q 'overlay2'; then echo "overlay2 storage driver supported"; else echo "overlay2 storage driver not detected"; fi; \
      else \
        echo "docker command not found, skipping overlay2 check"; \
      fi || true
  # Set default shell to bash and launch interactive CLI at container start
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 9 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONIOENCODING=utf-8
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get upgrade -y && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
        curl \
        jq \
        python3 \
        python3-pip \
        ca-certificates \
        git \
        lsb-release \
        sudo \
        bash \
        build-essential \
        wget \
        tar && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install gum (fixed version, robust extraction)
  RUN set -ex && \
      GUM_VERSION="v0.13.0" && \
      ARCH=amd64 && \
      GUM_FILENAME="gum_${GUM_VERSION#v}_linux_${ARCH}.tar.gz" && \
      GUM_URL="https://github.com/charmbracelet/gum/releases/download/${GUM_VERSION}/${GUM_FILENAME}" && \
      wget -O gum.tar.gz "$GUM_URL" && \
      tar -xzf gum.tar.gz && \
      find . -type f -name gum -exec mv {} /usr/local/bin/gum \; && \
      chmod +x /usr/local/bin/gum && \
      /usr/local/bin/gum --version && \
      rm -rf gum.tar.gz gum_${GUM_VERSION#v}_linux_${ARCH} gum_${GUM_VERSION#v}_linux_${ARCH}.tar.gz
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set working directory to repository root
  WORKDIR /nesa_bootstrap
  # Copy repository contents (assumes Docker build context is repository root)
  COPY . .
  # Download Nesa bootstrap script and make it executable
  RUN curl -O https://raw.githubusercontent.com/nesaorg/bootstrap/master/bootstrap.sh && \
      chmod +x bootstrap.sh
  # Create necessary directories for Nesa environment and logs
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.nesa/env /root/.nesa/logs
  # Ensure overlay2 storage driver is used if available (for tests, not enforced)
  RUN if command -v docker >/dev/null 2>&1; then \
        if docker info | grep -q 'overlay2'; then echo "overlay2 storage driver supported"; else echo "overlay2 storage driver not detected"; fi; \
      else \
        echo "docker command not found, skipping overlay2 check"; \
      fi || true
  # Set default shell to bash and launch interactive CLI at container start
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONIOENCODING=utf-8
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get upgrade -y && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
        curl \
        jq \
        python3 \
        python3-pip \
        ca-certificates \
        git \
        lsb-release \
        sudo \
        bash \
        build-essential \
        wget \
        tar && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install gum (fixed version, robust extraction)
  RUN set -ex && \
      GUM_VERSION="v0.13.0" && \
      ARCH=amd64 && \
      GUM_FILENAME="gum_${GUM_VERSION#v}_linux_${ARCH}.tar.gz" && \
      GUM_URL="https://github.com/charmbracelet/gum/releases/download/${GUM_VERSION}/${GUM_FILENAME}" && \
      wget -O gum.tar.gz "$GUM_URL" && \
      tar -xzf gum.tar.gz && \
      mv gum_${GUM_VERSION#v}_linux_${ARCH}/gum /usr/local/bin/gum && \
      chmod +x /usr/local/bin/gum && \
      /usr/local/bin/gum --version && \
      rm -rf gum.tar.gz gum_${GUM_VERSION#v}_linux_${ARCH}
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set working directory to repository root
  WORKDIR /nesa_bootstrap
  # Copy repository contents (assumes Docker build context is repository root)
  COPY . .
  # Download Nesa bootstrap script and make it executable
  RUN curl -O https://raw.githubusercontent.com/nesaorg/bootstrap/master/bootstrap.sh && \
      chmod +x bootstrap.sh
  # Create necessary directories for Nesa environment and logs
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.nesa/env /root/.nesa/logs
  # Ensure overlay2 storage driver is used if available (for tests, not enforced)
  RUN if command -v docker >/dev/null 2>&1; then \
        if docker info | grep -q 'overlay2'; then echo "overlay2 storage driver supported"; else echo "overlay2 storage driver not detected"; fi; \
      else \
        echo "docker command not found, skipping overlay2 check"; \
      fi || true
  # Set default shell to bash and launch interactive CLI at container start
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONIOENCODING=utf-8
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get upgrade -y && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
        curl \
        jq \
        python3 \
        python3-pip \
        ca-certificates \
        git \
        lsb-release \
        sudo \
        bash \
        build-essential \
        wget \
        tar && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install gum (fixed version, robust extraction)
  RUN set -ex && \
      GUM_VERSION="v0.13.0" && \
      ARCH=amd64 && \
      GUM_FILENAME="gum_${GUM_VERSION#v}_linux_${ARCH}.tar.gz" && \
      GUM_URL="https://github.com/charmbracelet/gum/releases/download/${GUM_VERSION}/${GUM_FILENAME}" && \
      wget -O gum.tar.gz "$GUM_URL" && \
      tar -xzf gum.tar.gz && \
      ls -l && \
      find . -type f -name gum -exec mv {} /usr/local/bin/gum \; && \
      chmod +x /usr/local/bin/gum && \
      /usr/local/bin/gum --version && \
      rm -rf gum.tar.gz gum*
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set working directory to repository root
  WORKDIR /nesa_bootstrap
  # Copy repository contents (assumes Docker build context is repository root)
  COPY . .
  # Download Nesa bootstrap script and make it executable
  RUN curl -O https://raw.githubusercontent.com/nesaorg/bootstrap/master/bootstrap.sh && \
      chmod +x bootstrap.sh
  # Create necessary directories for Nesa environment and logs
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.nesa/env /root/.nesa/logs
  # Ensure overlay2 storage driver is used if available (for tests, not enforced)
  RUN if command -v docker >/dev/null 2>&1; then \
        if docker info | grep -q 'overlay2'; then echo "overlay2 storage driver supported"; else echo "overlay2 storage driver not detected"; fi; \
      else \
        echo "docker command not found, skipping overlay2 check"; \
      fi || true
  # Set default shell to bash and launch interactive CLI at container start
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONIOENCODING=utf-8
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get upgrade -y && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
        curl \
        jq \
        python3 \
        python3-pip \
        ca-certificates \
        git \
        lsb-release \
        sudo \
        bash \
        build-essential \
        wget \
        tar && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install gum (fixed version, robust extraction with tarball structure detection)
  RUN set -ex && \
      GUM_VERSION="v0.13.0" && \
      ARCH=amd64 && \
      GUM_FILENAME="gum_${GUM_VERSION#v}_linux_${ARCH}.tar.gz" && \
      GUM_URL="https://github.com/charmbracelet/gum/releases/download/${GUM_VERSION}/${GUM_FILENAME}" && \
      wget -O gum.tar.gz "$GUM_URL" && \
      tar -tzf gum.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf gum.tar.gz && \
      mv gum*/gum /usr/local/bin/gum && \
      chmod +x /usr/local/bin/gum && \
      /usr/local/bin/gum --version && \
      rm -rf gum.tar.gz gum*
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set working directory to repository root
  WORKDIR /nesa_bootstrap
  # Copy repository contents (assumes Docker build context is repository root)
  COPY . .
  # Download Nesa bootstrap script and make it executable
  RUN curl -O https://raw.githubusercontent.com/nesaorg/bootstrap/master/bootstrap.sh && \
      chmod +x bootstrap.sh
  # Create necessary directories for Nesa environment and logs
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.nesa/env /root/.nesa/logs
  # Ensure overlay2 storage driver is used if available (for tests, not enforced)
  RUN if command -v docker >/dev/null 2>&1; then \
        if docker info | grep -q 'overlay2'; then echo "overlay2 storage driver supported"; else echo "overlay2 storage driver not detected"; fi; \
      else \
        echo "docker command not found, skipping overlay2 check"; \
      fi || true
  # Set default shell to bash and launch interactive CLI at container start
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

      find . -type f -name gum -exec mv {} /usr/local/bin/gum \; && \
      chmod +x /usr/local/bin/gum && \
      /usr/local/bin/gum --version && \
      rm -rf gum.tar.gz gum_*
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set working directory to repository root
  WORKDIR /nesa_bootstrap
  # Copy repository contents (assumes Docker build context is repository root)
  COPY . .
  # Download Nesa bootstrap script and make it executable
  RUN curl -O https://raw.githubusercontent.com/nesaorg/bootstrap/master/bootstrap.sh && \
      chmod +x bootstrap.sh
  # Create necessary directories for Nesa environment and logs
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.nesa/env /root/.nesa/logs
  # Ensure overlay2 storage driver is used if available (for tests, not enforced)
  RUN if command -v docker >/dev/null 2>&1; then \
        if docker info | grep -q 'overlay2'; then echo "overlay2 storage driver supported"; else echo "overlay2 storage driver not detected"; fi; \
      else \
        echo "docker command not found, skipping overlay2 check"; \
      fi || true
  # Set default shell to bash and launch interactive CLI at container start
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 16 ---

  next step
  - Fix the gum installation step in the Dockerfile:
    - The extraction and move command assumes the tarball extracts to a directory named "gum_0.13.0_linux_amd64", but the actual structure may differ.
    - Add a `tar -tzf gum.tar.gz` step to inspect the tarball contents before extracting/moving, or use a wildcard in the `mv` statement (e.g., `mv */gum /usr/local/bin/gum`).
    - Alternatively, extract and move the binary with a more robust pattern:
      ```
      tar -xzf gum.tar.gz
      find . -type f -name gum -exec mv {} /usr/local/bin/gum \;
      ```
    - Rebuild the Docker image to confirm successful gum installation and proceed with the rest of the steps.

  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONIOENCODING=utf-8
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get upgrade -y && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
        curl \
        jq \
        python3 \
        python3-pip \
        ca-certificates \
        git \
        lsb-release \
        sudo \
        bash \
        build-essential \
        wget \
        tar && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install gum (fixed version, robust extraction with tarball structure detection)
  RUN set -ex && \
      GUM_VERSION="v0.13.0" && \
      ARCH=amd64 && \
      GUM_FILENAME="gum_${GUM_VERSION#v}_linux_${ARCH}.tar.gz" && \
      GUM_URL="https://github.com/charmbracelet/gum/releases/download/${GUM_VERSION}/${GUM_FILENAME}" && \
      wget -O gum.tar.gz "$GUM_URL" && \
      tar -xzf gum.tar.gz && \
      mv "gum_${GUM_VERSION#v}_linux_${ARCH}/gum" /usr/local/bin/gum && \
      chmod +x /usr/local/bin/gum && \
      /usr/local/bin/gum --version && \
      rm -rf gum.tar.gz "gum_${GUM_VERSION#v}_linux_${ARCH}"
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set working directory to repository root
  WORKDIR /nesa_bootstrap
  # Copy repository contents (assumes Docker build context is repository root)
  COPY . .
  # Download Nesa bootstrap script and make it executable
  RUN curl -O https://raw.githubusercontent.com/nesaorg/bootstrap/master/bootstrap.sh && \
      chmod +x bootstrap.sh
  # Create necessary directories for Nesa environment and logs
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.nesa/env /root/.nesa/logs
  # Ensure overlay2 storage driver is used if available (for tests, not enforced)
  RUN if command -v docker >/dev/null 2>&1; then \
        if docker info | grep -q 'overlay2'; then echo "overlay2 storage driver supported"; else echo "overlay2 storage driver not detected"; fi; \
      else \
        echo "docker command not found, skipping overlay2 check"; \
      fi || true
  # Set default shell to bash and launch interactive CLI at container start
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONIOENCODING=utf-8
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get upgrade -y && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
        curl \
        jq \
        python3 \
        python3-pip \
        ca-certificates \
        git \
        lsb-release \
        sudo \
        bash \
        build-essential \
        wget \
        tar && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install gum (fixed version, robust extraction with tarball structure detection)
  RUN set -ex && \
      GUM_VERSION="v0.13.0" && \
      ARCH=amd64 && \
      GUM_FILENAME="gum_${GUM_VERSION#v}_linux_${ARCH}.tar.gz" && \
      GUM_URL="https://github.com/charmbracelet/gum/releases/download/${GUM_VERSION}/${GUM_FILENAME}" && \
      wget -O gum.tar.gz "$GUM_URL" && \
      tar -tzf gum.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf gum.tar.gz && \
      find . -type f -name gum -exec mv {} /usr/local/bin/gum \; && \
      chmod +x /usr/local/bin/gum && \
      /usr/local/bin/gum --version && \
      rm -rf gum.tar.gz gum_*_linux_${ARCH}
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set working directory to repository root
  WORKDIR /nesa_bootstrap
  # Copy repository contents (assumes Docker build context is repository root)
  COPY . .
  # Download Nesa bootstrap script and make it executable
  RUN curl -O https://raw.githubusercontent.com/nesaorg/bootstrap/master/bootstrap.sh && \
      chmod +x bootstrap.sh
  # Create necessary directories for Nesa environment and logs
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.nesa/env /root/.nesa/logs
  # Ensure overlay2 storage driver is used if available (for tests, not enforced)
  RUN if command -v docker >/dev/null 2>&1; then \
        if docker info | grep -q 'overlay2'; then echo "overlay2 storage driver supported"; else echo "overlay2 storage driver not detected"; fi; \
      else \
        echo "docker command not found, skipping overlay2 check"; \
      fi || true
  # Set default shell to bash and launch interactive CLI at container start
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONIOENCODING=utf-8
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get upgrade -y && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
        curl \
        jq \
        python3 \
        python3-pip \
        ca-certificates \
        git \
        lsb-release \
        sudo \
        bash \
        build-essential \
        wget \
        tar && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install gum (fixed version, robust extraction with direct move and cleanup)
  RUN set -ex && \
      GUM_VERSION="v0.13.0" && \
      ARCH=amd64 && \
      GUM_FILENAME="gum_${GUM_VERSION#v}_linux_${ARCH}.tar.gz" && \
      GUM_URL="https://github.com/charmbracelet/gum/releases/download/${GUM_VERSION}/${GUM_FILENAME}" && \
      wget -O gum.tar.gz "$GUM_URL" && \
      tar -xzf gum.tar.gz && \
      mv gum_*_linux_${ARCH}/gum /usr/local/bin/gum && \
      chmod +x /usr/local/bin/gum && \
      /usr/local/bin/gum --version && \
      rm -rf gum.tar.gz gum_*_linux_${ARCH}
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Set working directory to repository root
  WORKDIR /nesa_bootstrap
  # Copy repository contents (assumes Docker build context is repository root)
  COPY . .
  # Download Nesa bootstrap script and make it executable
  RUN curl -O https://raw.githubusercontent.com/nesaorg/bootstrap/master/bootstrap.sh && \
      chmod +x bootstrap.sh
  # Create necessary directories for Nesa environment and logs
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.nesa/env /root/.nesa/logs
  # Ensure overlay2 storage driver is used if available (for tests, not enforced)
  RUN if command -v docker >/dev/null 2>&1; then \
        if docker info | grep -q 'overlay2'; then echo "overlay2 storage driver supported"; else echo "overlay2 storage driver not detected"; fi; \
      else \
        echo "docker command not found, skipping overlay2 check"; \
      fi || true
  # Set default shell to bash and launch interactive CLI at container start
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
